<h1 data-id="heading-1">二、可选链（Optional Chaining）</h1>
<p>看下面的示例代码:</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> name: <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> dog: <span class="hljs-type">Dog</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Dog</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> car: <span class="hljs-type">Car</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Car</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">    </span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">age</span>() -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-number">18</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7">    </span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">eat</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person eat"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">    </span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { index }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">} </span>
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>如果可选项为<code>nil</code>，调用方法、下标、属性失败，结果为<code>nil</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> person: <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.age()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> name <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.name</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> index <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>[<span class="hljs-number">6</span>]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(age, name, index) <span class="hljs-comment">// nil, nil, nil </span></span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-comment">// 如果person为nil，都不会调用getName</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>() -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">String</span> { <span class="hljs-string">"jack"</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> person: <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.name <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> getName() </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>如果可选项不为<code>nil</code>，调用<code>方法</code>、<code>下标</code>、<code>属性</code>成功，结果会被包装成<code>可选项</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> person: <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.age()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> name <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.name</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> index <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>[<span class="hljs-number">6</span>]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(age, name, index) <span class="hljs-comment">// Optional(18) Optional("") Optional(6) </span></span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>如果结果<code>本来就是可选项</code>，不会进行再次包装</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.car) <span class="hljs-comment">// Optional(test_enum.Car) </span></span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">
<li>可以用可选绑定来判断可选项的方法调用是否成功</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> result: ()<span class="hljs-operator">?</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.eat()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> result {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"调用成功"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"调用失败"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">} </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.age() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"调用成功"</span>, age)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"调用失败"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="5">
<li>没有设定返回值的方法默认返回的就是<code>元组类型</code>
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/b8b75b19c58c4059a2380e609ddb9540~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w521" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="6">
<li>多个?可以连接在一起，组成可选链</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> dog <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.dog</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> weight <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.dog.weight</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> price <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> person<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.car<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.price </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="7">
<li>可选链中不管中间经历多少层，只要有一个节点是可选项的，那么最后的结果就是会被包装成可选项的</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(dog, weight, price) <span class="hljs-comment">// Optional(test_enum.Dog) Optional(0) Optional(0)</span></span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="8">
<li>如果链中任何一个节点是<code>nil</code>，那么整个链就会调用失败<br>
看下面示例代码</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> num1: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">5</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">num1<span class="hljs-operator">?</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(num1)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> num2: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">num2<span class="hljs-operator">?</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(num2) </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="9">
<li>给变量加上<code>?</code>是为了判断变量是否为<code>nil</code>，如果为<code>nil</code>，那么就不会执行赋值操作了，本质也是可选链</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> dict: [<span class="hljs-type">String</span> : (<span class="hljs-type">Int</span>, <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>] <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-string">"sum"</span> : (<span class="hljs-operator">+</span>),</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-string">"difference"</span> : (<span class="hljs-operator">-</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> value <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> dict[<span class="hljs-string">"sum"</span>]<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">20</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(value) </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
</ul>
<p>从字典中通过key来取值，得到的也是可选类型，由于可选链中有一个节点是可选项，那么最后的结果也是可选项，最后的值也是<code>Int?</code></p>
<h1 data-id="heading-2">三、协议（Protocol）</h1>
<h2 data-id="heading-3">1. 基本概念</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li><code>协议</code>可以用来定义<code>方法</code>、<code>属性</code>、<code>下标</code>的声明<br>
<code>协议</code>可以被<code>结构体</code>、<code>类</code>、<code>枚举</code>遵守</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> x: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> } <span class="hljs-comment">// get和set只是声明</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> y: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>多个协议</code>之间用逗号隔开</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Test1</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Test2</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Test3</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">TestClass</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Test1</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Test2</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Test3</span> { } </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>协议中定义方法时不能有默认参数值
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/f7119b8167f647fe819d6285c3c57f9f~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w633" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">
<li>默认情况下，协议中定义的内容必须全部都实现</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-4">2. 协议中的属性</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li><code>协议</code>中定义属性必须用<code>var</code>关键字</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>实现<code>协议</code>时的属性权限要不小于<code>协议</code>中定义的<code>属性权限</code></li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>协议定义<code>get、set</code>，用<code>var</code>存储属性或<code>get、set</code>计算属性去实现</li>
<li>协议定义<code>get</code>，用任何属性都可以实现</li>
</ul>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> x: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> y: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> x: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> y: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person1 draw"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17">        <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18">        <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> { index }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="20">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="21"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="22"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="23">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> x: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="24">        <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> { <span class="hljs-number">0</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="25">        <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="26">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="27"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="28">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> y: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> { <span class="hljs-number">0</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="29"></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="31">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person2 draw"</span>)</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="34">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="52">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person3 draw"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="53">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="54"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="55">    <span class="hljs-keyword">subscript</span>(<span class="hljs-params">index</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="58">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="59">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-5">3. static、class</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>为了保证通用，<code>协议</code>中必须用<code>static</code>定义<code>类型方法</code>、<code>类型属性</code>、<code>类型下标</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person1 draw"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">func</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">draw</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Person2 draw"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-6">4. mutating</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>只有将<code>协议</code>中的<code>实例方法</code>标记为<code>mutating</code>，才允许<code>结构体</code>、<code>枚举</code>的具体实现修改自身内存</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>类</code>在实现方法时不用加<code>mutating</code>，<code>结构体</code>、<code>枚举</code>才需要加<code>mutating</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">mutating</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Size</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> width: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">        width <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> x: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">    <span class="hljs-keyword">mutating</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16">        x <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-7">5. init</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>协议中还可以定义初始化器<code>init</code>，非<code>final</code>类实现时必须加上<code>required</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>目的是为了让所有遵守这个协议的类都拥有初始化器，所以加上<code>required</code>强制子类必须实现，除非是加上<code>final</code>不需要子类的类</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>, <span class="hljs-params">y</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">required</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>, <span class="hljs-params">y</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"><span class="hljs-keyword">final</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Size</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Drawable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>, <span class="hljs-params">y</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>如果从协议实现的初始化器，刚好是重写了父类的指定初始化器，那么这个初始化必须同时加上<code>required、override</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Livable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">age</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">age</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Student</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Livable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    <span class="hljs-keyword">required</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">override</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">init</span>(<span class="hljs-params">age</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">

</li>

<h2 data-id="heading-8">6. 协议的继承</h2>
<p>一个<code>协议</code>可以继承其他协议</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Livable</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">breath</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Livable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">breath</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17">} </span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-9">7. 协议组合</h2>
<p>协议组合可以包含一个类类型</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Livable</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-comment">// 接收Person或者其子类的实例</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fn0</span>(<span class="hljs-params">obj</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>) { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-comment">// 接收遵守Livable协议的实例</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fn1</span>(<span class="hljs-params">obj</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Livable</span>) { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"><span class="hljs-comment">// 接收同时遵守Livable、Runnable协议的实例</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fn2</span>(<span class="hljs-params">obj</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Livable</span> &amp; <span class="hljs-type">Runnable</span>) { }</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17"><span class="hljs-keyword">typealias</span> <span class="hljs-type">RealPerson</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span> &amp; <span class="hljs-type">Livable</span> &amp; <span class="hljs-type">Runnable</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fn4</span>(<span class="hljs-params">obj</span>: <span class="hljs-type">RealPerson</span>) { } </span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-10">8. CaseIterable</h2>
<p>让枚举遵守<code>CaseIterable</code>协议，可以实现遍历枚举值</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Season</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">CaseIterable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> spring, summer, autumn, winter</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> seasons <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Season</span>.allCases</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(seasons.count)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> season <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> seasons {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(season)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">} <span class="hljs-comment">// spring, summer, autumn, winter </span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-11">9.CustomStringConvertible</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>遵守<code>CustomStringConvertible、CustomDebugStringConvertible</code>协议，都可以自定义实例的打印字符串</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">CustomStringConvertible</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">CustomDebugStringConvertible</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> description: <span class="hljs-type">String</span> { <span class="hljs-string">"person_(age)"</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> debugDescription: <span class="hljs-type">String</span> { <span class="hljs-string">"debug_person_(age)"</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> person <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(person) <span class="hljs-comment">// person_0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-built_in">debugPrint</span>(person) <span class="hljs-comment">// debug_person_0 </span></span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>print</code>调用的是<code>CustomStringConvertible</code>协议的<code>description</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li><code>debugPrint、po</code>调用的是<code>CustomDebugStringConvertible</code>协议的<code>debugDescription</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/acc8277e7aa14a60a23a27f52a4b11fc~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w529" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></p>
<h1 data-id="heading-12">四、Any、AnyObject与元类型</h1>
<h2 data-id="heading-13">1. Any、AnyObject</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>Swift提供了两种特殊的类型<code>Any、AnyObject</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>Any</code>可以代表任意类型（<code>枚举</code>、<code>结构体</code>、<code>类</code>，也包括<code>函数类型</code>）</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> stu: <span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">stu <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"Jack"</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">stu <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Size</span>() </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> data <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span>]()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">data.append(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">data.append(<span class="hljs-number">3.14</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">data.append(<span class="hljs-type">Size</span>())</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">data.append(<span class="hljs-string">"Jack"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">data.append({ <span class="hljs-number">10</span> }) </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li><code>AnyObject</code>可以代表任意类类型</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">
<li>在协议后面写上<code>: AnyObject</code>，代表只有类能遵守这个协议
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/d3809ed07d17450d911eec4ad2731c0f~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w644" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="5">
<li>在协议后面写上<code>: class</code>，也代表只有类能遵守这个协议
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/c3c89cc874464f83a7bdb5c65a31b83c~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w642" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-14">2. is、as</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>is</code>用来判断是否为某种类型
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Student</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Student run"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">study</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Student study"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> stu: <span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="20">stu <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"Jack"</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="21"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="22"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="23">stu <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Student</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="24"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="25"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">Student</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="26"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">Runnable</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// true </span></span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>as</code>用来做强制类型转换(<code>as?</code>、<code>as!</code>、<code>as</code>)</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> { }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Student</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Runnable</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Student run"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">    <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">study</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">        <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Student study"</span>)</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> stu: <span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19"></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="21">(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">as?</span> <span class="hljs-type">Student</span>)<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.study() <span class="hljs-comment">// Student study</span></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="23">(stu <span class="hljs-keyword">as?</span> <span class="hljs-type">Runnable</span>)<span class="hljs-operator">?</span>.run() <span class="hljs-comment">// Student run </span></span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> data <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span>]()</span>

</code></pre>

</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-15">3. X.self</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li><code>X.self</code>是一个<code>元类型的指针</code>，<code>metadata</code>存放着<code>类型相关信息</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>X.self</code>属于<code>X.Type</code>类型</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> { }</span>

<h2 data-id="heading-17">5. Self</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li><code>Self</code>代表当前类型</li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">1</span></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">    }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">} </span>
</code></pre>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">

</ol>

</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-18">6. 元类型的本质</h2>
<p>我们可以通过反汇编来查看元类型的实现是怎样的</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> p <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> pType <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>.<span class="hljs-keyword">self</span> </span>
</code></pre>
<p>我们发现最后存储到全局变量pType中的地址值就是一开始调用的地址
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/8a38e68565b04a649793fd49e4962bc8~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w1031" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image">
再通过打印，我们发现pType的值就是Person实例对象的前8个字节的地址值，也就是类信息
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/f81fff9375c949a18a6e71f733e06da5~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w1031" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image">
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/d84b816435c0422a9ea5bfde95b40861~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w1032" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image">
我们再来看下面的示例代码</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> p <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-type">Person</span>()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> pType <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">type</span>(of: p) </span>
</code></pre>
<p>通过分析我们可以看到<code>type(of: p)</code>本质不是函数调用，只是将Person实例对象的前8个字节存储到pType中，也证明了元类型的本质就是存储的类信息</p>
<p><img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/f11a754847b149eab14026ed50e0ff21~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w1031" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image">
<img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/aa877aa499e7423e86c1e96bd301d291~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w1030" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></p>
<p>我们还可以用以下方式来获取Swift的隐藏基类<code>_TtCs12_SwiftObject</code></p>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Student</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> no: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7">}</span>
