</code></pre>
<h1 data-id="heading-89">十四、模式匹配（Pattern）</h1>
<h2 data-id="heading-90">1. 基本概念</h2>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>什么是模式？</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>模式是用于匹配的规则，比如<code>switch的case、捕捉错误的catch、if\guard\while\for语句的条件</code>等</li>
</ul>
<p>Swift中的模式有</p>
<ul>
<li>通配符模式（Wildcard Pattern）</li>
<li>标识符模式（Identifier Pattern）</li>
<li>值绑定模式（Value-Binding Pattern）</li>
<li>元组模式（Tuple Pattern）</li>
<li>枚举Case模式（Enumeration Case Pattern）</li>
<li>可选模式（Optional Pattern）</li>
<li>类型转换模式（Type-Casting Pattern）</li>
<li>表达式模式（Expression Pattern）</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-id="heading-91">2. 通配符模式（Wildcard Pattern）</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>_</code>匹配任何值</li>
<li><code>_?</code>匹配非<code>nil</code>值</li>
</ul>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Life</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> human(name: <span class="hljs-type">String</span>, age: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> animal(name: <span class="hljs-type">String</span>, age: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">check</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">_</span> <span class="hljs-params">life</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Life</span>) {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> life {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> .human(<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> name, <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span>):</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"human"</span>, name)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> .animal(<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> name, <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span><span class="hljs-operator">?</span>):</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"animal"</span>, name)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"other"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17">check(.human(name: <span class="hljs-string">"Rose"</span>, age: <span class="hljs-number">20</span>)) <span class="hljs-comment">// human Rose</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18">check(.human(name: <span class="hljs-string">"Jack"</span>, age: <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>)) <span class="hljs-comment">// human Jack</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19">check(.animal(name: <span class="hljs-string">"Dog"</span>, age: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>)) <span class="hljs-comment">// animal Dog</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="20">check(.animal(name: <span class="hljs-string">"Cat"</span>, age: <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>)) <span class="hljs-comment">// other</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-92">2.标识符模式（Identifier Pattern）</h2>
<p>给对应的变量、常量名赋值</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> name <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"jack"</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-93">3.值绑定模式（Value-Binding Pattern）</h2>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> point <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> (<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> point {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> (x, y):</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"The point is at ((x), (y)."</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">} </span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-94">4.元组模式（Tuple Pattern）</h2>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> points <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (x, <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> points {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(x)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">} </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> name: <span class="hljs-type">String</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"jack"</span></span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">} <span class="hljs-comment">// default </span></span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> scores <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-string">"jack"</span> : <span class="hljs-number">98</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"rose"</span> : <span class="hljs-number">100</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"kate"</span> : <span class="hljs-number">86</span>]</span>

</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-95">5. 枚举Case模式（Enumeration Case Pattern）</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>if case</code>语句等价于只有1个<code>case</code>的<code>switch</code>语句</li>
</ul>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-comment">// 原来的写法</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">&gt;=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span> <span class="hljs-operator">&amp;&amp;</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">&lt;=</span> <span class="hljs-number">9</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"[0, 9]"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-comment">// 枚举Case模式</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span><span class="hljs-operator">...</span><span class="hljs-number">9</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> age {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"[0, 9]"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13"><span class="hljs-keyword">guard</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span><span class="hljs-operator">...</span><span class="hljs-number">9</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> age <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"[0, 9]"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16"><span class="hljs-comment">// 等同于switch case</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> age {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span><span class="hljs-operator">...</span><span class="hljs-number">9</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"[0, 9]"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="20">} </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> ages: [<span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?] <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> ages {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"有nil值"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">} <span class="hljs-comment">// 有nil值 </span></span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> points <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)]</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(x)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">} <span class="hljs-comment">// 1 3 </span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-96">6. 可选模式（Optional Pattern）</h2>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> age: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>? <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">42</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> .some(<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> x) <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> age { <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(x) }</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> x<span class="hljs-operator">?</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> age { <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(x) }</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> ages: [<span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?] <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> age<span class="hljs-operator">?</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> ages {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(age)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">} <span class="hljs-comment">// 2 3 5</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-comment">// 同上面效果等价</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> ages: [<span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?] <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> item <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> ages {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(age)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12">}  </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">check</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">_</span> <span class="hljs-params">num</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>?) {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span><span class="hljs-operator">?</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"2"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">4</span><span class="hljs-operator">?</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"4"</span>)</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span><span class="hljs-operator">?</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"other"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"nil"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">}</span>

<h2 data-id="heading-97">7.类型转换模式（Type-Casting Pattern）</h2>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> num: <span class="hljs-keyword">Any</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">6</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> num {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-comment">// 编译器依然认为num是Any类型</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"is Int"</span>, num)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-comment">//case let n as Int:</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-comment">//    print("as Int", n + 1)</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9"><span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">} </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5">}</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">run</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-built_in">type</span>(of: <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>), <span class="hljs-string">"run"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="10">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="11">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="12"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="13"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="14"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">jump</span>() {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="15">    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-built_in">type</span>(of: <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>), <span class="hljs-string">"jump"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="16">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="17">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="18"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="19"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">check</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">_</span> <span class="hljs-params">animal</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Animal</span>) {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="20"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> animal {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="21"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> dog <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> <span class="hljs-type">Dog</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="22">    dog.eat()</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="23">    dog.run()</span>

<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="26"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="27">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="28">}</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="29"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="30">check(<span class="hljs-type">Dog</span>()) <span class="hljs-comment">// Dog eat, Dog run</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="31">check(<span class="hljs-type">Cat</span>()) <span class="hljs-comment">// Cat eat </span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-98">8.表达式模式（Expression Pattern）</h2>
<p>表达式模式用在<code>case</code>中</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> point <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> point {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> (<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>):</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"(0, 0) is at the origin."</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> (<span class="hljs-operator">-</span><span class="hljs-number">2</span><span class="hljs-operator">...</span><span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-operator">-</span><span class="hljs-number">2</span><span class="hljs-operator">...</span><span class="hljs-number">2</span>):</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"((point.0), (point.1) is near the origin."</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"The point is at ((point.0), (point.1)."</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">} <span class="hljs-comment">// (1, 2) is near the origin. </span></span>
</code></pre>
<p>通过反汇编，我们可以看到其内部会调用<code>~=运算符</code>来计算<code>(-2...2, -2...2)</code>这个区间</p>
<p><img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/5e9c12335d5e4f01bac6820368e90f2b~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp" alt="-w714" loading="lazy" class="medium-zoom-image"></p>
<h2 data-id="heading-99">9. 自定义表达式模式</h2>
<p>可以通过重载运算符，自定义表达式模式的匹配规则</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Student</span> {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> score <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, name <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-comment">// pattern：放的是case后面的值</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-comment">// value：放的是switch后面的值</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">~=</span> (<span class="hljs-params">pattern</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Int</span>, <span class="hljs-params">value</span>: <span class="hljs-type">Student</span>) -&gt; <span class="hljs-type">Bool</span> {</span>

<h2 data-id="heading-100">10. where</h2>
<p>可以使用<code>where</code>为模式匹配增加匹配条件</p>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> data <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> (<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Jack"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="2"><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> data {</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="3"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> (age, <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">where</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-number">10</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="4"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(data.<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"age&gt;10"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="5"><span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> (age, <span class="hljs-keyword">_</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">where</span> age <span class="hljs-operator">&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="6"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(data.<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"age&gt;0"</span>)</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="7"><span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:</span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="8"><span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span>
<span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="9">} </span>
</code></pre>
<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> ages <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> [<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">20</span>, <span class="hljs-number">44</span>, <span class="hljs-number">23</span>, <span class="hljs-number">55</span>]</span>

<pre><div class="code-block-extension-header" style="background-color: rgb(248, 248, 248);"><div class="code-block-extension-headerLeft"><div class="code-block-extension-foldBtn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M16.924 9.617A1 1 0 0 0 16 9H8a1 1 0 0 0-.707 1.707l4 4a1 1 0 0 0 1.414 0l4-4a1 1 0 0 0 .217-1.09z" data-name="Down"></path></svg></div></div><div class="code-block-extension-headerRight"><span class="code-block-extension-lang">swift</span><div class="code-block-extension-copyCodeBtn">复制代码</div></div></div><code class="hljs language-swift code-block-extension-codeShowNum" lang="swift"><span class="code-block-extension-codeLine" data-line-num="1"><span class="hljs-keyword">protocol</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Stackable</span> {</span>
